quarter earnings in fiscal year 2023.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">Revenues were $11.4 billion, compared to $12.8 billion in the first quarter of fiscal year 2023.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">Our Energy segment experienced favorable market conditions in our refined fuels business, reflecting sustained global demand for energy products.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">In our Ag segment, continued robust meal and oil demand drove strong earnings in our oilseed processing business that were offset by weak U.S. export demand for grains and oilseeds.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.15pt">Equity method investments performed well, with our CF Nitrogen investment being the largest contributor.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;CHS earnings were strong for the first quarter, despite a relative decline from last year's record earnings,&#8221; said Jay Debertin, president and CEO of CHS Inc. &#8220;Our focus on execution and efficiency improvements bolstered results across all operations. We continue to see the benefits of our diversified ag and energy portfolio, our strategic footprint and investments in our supply chain. The success of our domestic soybean and canola processing business and our international origination capabilities have helped us add value to our farmer-owners' businesses.&#34;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Energy </font></div><div><font trade flows returning to more normal levels</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">CHS Inc. (</font><font style="color:#3051f2;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">www.chsinc.com</font><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">) creates connections to empower agriculture. As a leading global agribusiness and the largest farmer-owned cooperative in the United States, CHS serves customers in 65 countries and employs nearly 10,000 people worldwide. We provide critical crop inputs, market access and risk management services that help farmers feed the world. Our diversified agronomy, grains, foods and energy businesses recorded revenues of $45.6 billion in fiscal year 2023. We advance sustainability through our commitment to being stewards of the environment, building economic viability and strengthening community and employee well-being. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This document and other CHS Inc. publicly available documents contain, and CHS officers, directors and representatives may from time to time make, &#34;forward-looking statements&#34; within the meaning of the safe harbor provisions of the U.S. Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995.
